         <div class="postcell post-layout--right">
          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            I have classes like these:
           </p>
           <pre><code>class MyDate
{
    int year, month, day;
}

class Lad
{
    string firstName;
    string lastName;
    MyDate dateOfBirth;
}
</code></pre>
           <p>
            And I would like to turn a
            <code>
             Lad
            </code>
            object into a
            <strong>
             JSON
            </strong>
            string like this:
           </p>
           <pre><code>{
    "firstName":"Markoff",
    "lastName":"Chaney",
    "dateOfBirth":
    {
        "year":"1901",
        "month":"4",
        "day":"30"
    }
}
</code></pre>
           <p>
            (Without the formatting). I found
            <a href="http://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/system.web.script.serialization.javascriptserializer(v=vs.110).aspx" rel="noreferrer">
             this link
            </a>
            , but it uses a namespace that's not in
            <strong>
             .NET 4
            </strong>
            . I also heard about
            <a href="http://james.newtonking.com/projects/json-net.aspx" rel="noreferrer">
             JSON.NET
            </a>
            , but their site seems to be down at the moment, and I'm not keen on using external DLL files.
           </p>
           <p>
            Are there other options besides manually creating a
            <strong>
             JSON
            </strong>
            string writer?
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="mt24 mb12">
           <div class="post-taglist d-flex gs4 gsy fd-column">
            <div class="d-flex ps-relative fw-wrap">

              serialization
             </a>
            </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              Since we all love one-liners
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             ... this one depends on the Newtonsoft NuGet package, which is popular and better than the default serializer.
            </p>
            <pre><code>Newtonsoft.Json.JsonConvert.SerializeObject(new {foo = "bar"})
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Documentation:
             <strong>
              <a href="http://www.newtonsoft.com/json/help/html/SerializingJSON.htm" rel="noreferrer">
               Serializing and Deserializing JSON
              </a>
             </strong>
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h2>
             Please Note
            </h2>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Microsoft recommends that you DO NOT USE JavaScriptSerializer
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             See the header of the documentation page:
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              For .NET Framework 4.7.2 and later versions, use the APIs in the System.Text.Json namespace for serialization and deserialization. For earlier versions of .NET Framework, use Newtonsoft.Json.
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <hr/>
            <h4>
             Original answer:
            </h4>
            <p>
             You could use the
             <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/api/system.web.script.serialization.javascriptserializer" rel="noreferrer">
              <code>
               JavaScriptSerializer
              </code>
             </a>
             class (add reference to
             <code>
              System.Web.Extensions
             </code>
             ):
            </p>
            <pre><code>using System.Web.Script.Serialization;
</code></pre>
            <pre><code>var json = new JavaScriptSerializer().Serialize(obj);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             A full example:
            </p>
            <pre><code>using System;
using System.Web.Script.Serialization;

public class MyDate
{
    public int year;
    public int month;
    public int day;
}

public class Lad
{
    public string firstName;
    public string lastName;
    public MyDate dateOfBirth;
}

class Program
{
    static void Main()
    {
        var obj = new Lad
        {
            firstName = "Markoff",
            lastName = "Chaney",
            dateOfBirth = new MyDate
            {
                year = 1901,
                month = 4,
                day = 30
            }
        };
        var json = new JavaScriptSerializer().Serialize(obj);
        Console.WriteLine(json);
    }
}
</code></pre>
           </div>

               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 <a href="http://csharp2json.azurewebsites.net/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  here
                 </a>
                 is
                 <b>
                  online tool
                 </b>
                 to convert your
                 <code>
                  classes
                 </code>
                 to
                 <code>
                  json
                 </code>
                 format, hope helps someone.
                </span>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="44670447" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6201529" data-position-on-page="3" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="127" id="answer-44670447" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="44670447">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="127" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             127
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/44670447/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Use
             <a href="http://www.newtonsoft.com/" rel="noreferrer">
              Json.Net
             </a>
             library, you can download it from Nuget Packet Manager.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Serializing to Json String:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code> var obj = new Lad
        {
            firstName = "Markoff",
            lastName = "Chaney",
            dateOfBirth = new MyDate
            {
                year = 1901,
                month = 4,
                day = 30
            }
        };

var jsonString = Newtonsoft.Json.JsonConvert.SerializeObject(obj);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Deserializing to Object:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>var obj = Newtonsoft.Json.JsonConvert.DeserializeObject&lt;Lad&gt;(jsonString );
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="6201579" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6201529" data-position-on-page="4" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="63" id="answer-6201579" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="6201579">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="63" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             63
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/6201579/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Use the
             <code>
              DataContractJsonSerializer
             </code>
             class:
             <a href="http://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/system.runtime.serialization.json.datacontractjsonserializer.aspx" rel="noreferrer">
              MSDN1
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="http://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/bb412179(v=vs.110).aspx" rel="noreferrer">
              MSDN2
             </a>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             My example:
             <a href="http://pastebin.com/8Wyn9K7F" rel="noreferrer">
              HERE
             </a>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             It can also safely deserialize objects from a JSON string, unlike
             <code>
              JavaScriptSerializer
             </code>
             . But personally I still prefer
             <a href="http://www.newtonsoft.com/json" rel="noreferrer">
              Json.NET
             </a>
             .
            </p>
           </div>

                  that page
                 </i>
                 , but here are some on
                 <a href="http://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/bb412179(v=vs.110).aspx" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  MSDN
                 </a>
                 and
                 <a href="http://www.joe-stevens.com/2009/12/29/json-serialization-using-the-datacontractjsonserializer-and-c/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  elsewhere
                 </a>
                 -&gt; the last one uses extension methods to achieve one-liners.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="58294305" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6201529" data-position-on-page="5" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="55" id="answer-58294305" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="58294305">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="55" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             55
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/58294305/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             A new JSON serializer is available in the
             <code>
              System.Text.Json
             </code>
             namespace. It's included in the .NET Core 3.0 shared framework and is in a
             <a href="https://www.nuget.org/packages/System.Text.Json" rel="noreferrer">
              NuGet package
             </a>
             for projects that target .NET Standard or .NET Framework or .NET Core 2.x.
            </p>
            <p>
             Example code:
            </p>
            <pre><code>using System;
using System.Text.Json;

public class MyDate
{
    public int year { get; set; }
    public int month { get; set; }
    public int day { get; set; }
}

public class Lad
{
    public string FirstName { get; set; }
    public string LastName { get; set; }
    public MyDate DateOfBirth { get; set; }
}

class Program
{
    static void Main()
    {
        var lad = new Lad
        {
            FirstName = "Markoff",
            LastName = "Chaney",
            DateOfBirth = new MyDate
            {
                year = 1901,
                month = 4,
                day = 30
            }
        };
        var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(lad);
        Console.WriteLine(json);
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             In this example the classes to be serialized have properties rather than fields; the
             <code>
              System.Text.Json
             </code>
             serializer currently doesn't serialize fields.
            </p>
            <p>
             Documentation:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/standard/serialization/system-text-json-overview" rel="noreferrer">
               System.Text.Json overview
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/standard/serialization/system-text-json-how-to" rel="noreferrer">
               How to use System.Text.Json
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="124554814" data-comment-owner-id="7586301" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-124554814">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Side notes: (1) in order to manage a json serialization the properties of the class must have at least getters, (2)
                 <code>
                  JsonSerializer.Serialize(lad)
                 </code>
                 prints all in one line; if you want to get an indented printout use the json
                 <code>
                  options
                 </code>
                 , (3) I would rather override
                 <code>
                  ToString()
                 </code>
                 in the class itself, so that you have never have to write again the whole
                 <code>
                  JsonSerializer.Serialize(lad)
                 </code>
                 sentence, just put inside the class this:
                 <code>
                  public override string ToString() =&gt; JsonSerializer.Serialize(this, new JsonSerializerOptions { WriteIndented = true });
                 </code>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/7586301/paul-efford" title="200 reputation">
                  Paul Efford
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2021-12-23 11:36:06Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0">
                  Dec 23, 2021 at 11:36
                 </span>
                </span>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You can achieve this by using Newtonsoft.json. Install Newtonsoft.json from NuGet. And then:
            </p>
            <pre><code>using Newtonsoft.Json;

var jsonString = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(obj);
</code></pre>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Wooou! Really better using a JSON framework :)
            </p>
            <p>
             Here is my example using Json.NET (
             <a href="http://james.newtonking.com/json">
              http://james.newtonking.com/json
             </a>
             ):
            </p>
            <pre><code>using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Text;
using Newtonsoft.Json;
using System.IO;

namespace com.blogspot.jeanjmichel.jsontest.model
{
    public class Contact
    {
        private Int64 id;
        private String name;
        List&lt;Address&gt; addresses;

        public Int64 Id
        {
            set { this.id = value; }
            get { return this.id; }
        }

        public String Name
        {
            set { this.name = value; }
            get { return this.name; }
        }

        public List&lt;Address&gt; Addresses
        {
            set { this.addresses = value; }
            get { return this.addresses; }
        }

        public String ToJSONRepresentation()
        {
            StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
            JsonWriter jw = new JsonTextWriter(new StringWriter(sb));

            jw.Formatting = Formatting.Indented;
            jw.WriteStartObject();
            jw.WritePropertyName("id");
            jw.WriteValue(this.Id);
            jw.WritePropertyName("name");
            jw.WriteValue(this.Name);

            jw.WritePropertyName("addresses");
            jw.WriteStartArray();

            int i;
            i = 0;

            for (i = 0; i &lt; addresses.Count; i++)
            {
                jw.WriteStartObject();
                jw.WritePropertyName("id");
                jw.WriteValue(addresses[i].Id);
                jw.WritePropertyName("streetAddress");
                jw.WriteValue(addresses[i].StreetAddress);
                jw.WritePropertyName("complement");
                jw.WriteValue(addresses[i].Complement);
                jw.WritePropertyName("city");
                jw.WriteValue(addresses[i].City);
                jw.WritePropertyName("province");
                jw.WriteValue(addresses[i].Province);
                jw.WritePropertyName("country");
                jw.WriteValue(addresses[i].Country);
                jw.WritePropertyName("postalCode");
                jw.WriteValue(addresses[i].PostalCode);
                jw.WriteEndObject();
            }

            jw.WriteEndArray();

            jw.WriteEndObject();

            return sb.ToString();
        }

        public Contact()
        {
        }

        public Contact(Int64 id, String personName, List&lt;Address&gt; addresses)
        {
            this.id = id;
            this.name = personName;
            this.addresses = addresses;
        }

        public Contact(String JSONRepresentation)
        {
            //To do
        }
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The test:
            </p>
            <pre><code>using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using com.blogspot.jeanjmichel.jsontest.model;

namespace com.blogspot.jeanjmichel.jsontest.main
{
    public class Program
    {
        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            List&lt;Address&gt; addresses = new List&lt;Address&gt;();
            addresses.Add(new Address(1, "Rua Dr. Fernandes Coelho, 85", "15º andar", "São Paulo", "São Paulo", "Brazil", "05423040"));
            addresses.Add(new Address(2, "Avenida Senador Teotônio Vilela, 241", null, "São Paulo", "São Paulo", "Brazil", null));

            Contact contact = new Contact(1, "Ayrton Senna", addresses);

            Console.WriteLine(contact.ToJSONRepresentation());
            Console.ReadKey();
        }
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The result:
            </p>
            <pre><code>{
  "id": 1,
  "name": "Ayrton Senna",
  "addresses": [
    {
      "id": 1,
      "streetAddress": "Rua Dr. Fernandes Coelho, 85",
      "complement": "15º andar",
      "city": "São Paulo",
      "province": "São Paulo",
      "country": "Brazil",
      "postalCode": "05423040"
    },
    {
      "id": 2,
      "streetAddress": "Avenida Senador Teotônio Vilela, 241",
      "complement": null,
      "city": "São Paulo",
      "province": "São Paulo",
      "country": "Brazil",
      "postalCode": null
    }
  ]
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Now I will implement the constructor method that will receives a JSON string and populates the class' fields.
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="48488304">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/48488304/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If they are not very big, what's probably your case export it as JSON.
            </p>
            <p>
             Also this makes it portable among all platforms.
            </p>
            <pre><code>using Newtonsoft.Json;

[TestMethod]
public void ExportJson()
{
    double[,] b = new double[,]
        {
            { 110,  120,  130,  140, 150 },
            {1110, 1120, 1130, 1140, 1150},
            {1000,    1,   5,     9, 1000},
            {1110,    2,   6,    10, 1110},
            {1220,    3,   7,    11, 1220},
            {1330,    4,   8,    12, 1330}
        };

    string jsonStr = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(b);

    Console.WriteLine(jsonStr);

    string path = "X:\\Programming\\workspaceEclipse\\PyTutorials\\src\\tensorflow_tutorials\\export.txt";

    File.WriteAllText(path, jsonStr);
}
</code></pre>
           </div>

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I would vote for ServiceStack's JSON Serializer:
            </p>
            <pre><code>using ServiceStack;

string jsonString = new { FirstName = "James" }.ToJson();
</code></pre>
            <p>
             It is also the fastest JSON serializer available for .NET:
             <a href="http://www.servicestack.net/benchmarks/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              http://www.servicestack.net/benchmarks/
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

             </time>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             It is as easy as this (it works for dynamic objects as well (type object)):
            </p>
            <pre><code>string json = new
System.Web.Script.Serialization.JavaScriptSerializer().Serialize(MYOBJECT);
</code></pre>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="66640112">

            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/66640112/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Another solution using
             <code>
              System.Text.Json
             </code>
             (.NET Core 3.0+, .NET 5) where an
             <strong>
              object is self-sufficient
             </strong>
             and doesn't expose all possible fields:
            </p>
            <p>
             A passing test:
            </p>
            <pre><code>using NUnit.Framework;

namespace Intech.UnitTests
{
    public class UserTests
    {
        [Test]
        public void ConvertsItselfToJson()
        {
            var userName = "John";
            var user = new User(userName);

            var actual = user.ToJson();

            Assert.AreEqual($"{{\"Name\":\"{userName}\"}}", actual);
        }
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             An implementation:
            </p>
            <pre><code>using System.Text.Json;
using System.Collections.Generic;

namespace Intech
{
    public class User
    {
        private readonly string Name;

        public User(string name)
        {
            this.Name = name;
        }

        public string ToJson()
        {
            var params = new Dictionary&lt;string, string&gt;{{"Name", Name}};
            return JsonSerializer.Serialize(params);
        }
    }
}
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="66192941" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6201529" data-position-on-page="13" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="1" id="answer-66192941" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="66192941">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/66192941/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             In your Lad model class, add an override to the
             <strong>
              ToString()
             </strong>
             method that returns a JSON string version of your Lad object.
             <br/>
             Note: you will need to import
             <strong>
              System.Text.Json
             </strong>
             ;
            </p>
            <pre><code>using System.Text.Json;

class MyDate
{
    int year, month, day;
}

class Lad
{
    public string firstName { get; set; };
    public string lastName { get; set; };
    public MyDate dateOfBirth { get; set; };
    public override string ToString() =&gt; JsonSerializer.Serialize&lt;Lad&gt;(this);
}
</code></pre>
           </div>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="124554915" data-comment-owner-id="7586301" data-comment-score="1" id="comment-124554915">

              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Side notes: (1) in order to manage a json serialization the properties of the class must have at least getters, (2)
                 <code>
                  JsonSerializer.Serialize(lad)
                 </code>
                 prints all in one line; if you want to get an indented printout use the json
                 <code>
                  options
                 </code>
                 , (3) I would rather override
                 <code>
                  ToString()
                 </code>
                 like this:
                 <code>
                  public override string ToString() =&gt; JsonSerializer.Serialize(this, new JsonSerializerOptions { WriteIndented = true });
                 </code>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/7586301/paul-efford" title="200 reputation">
                  Paul Efford
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2021-12-23 11:41:50Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0">
                  Dec 23, 2021 at 11:41
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Here is another solution using
             <a href="https://www.nuget.org/packages/ChoETL.JSON/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              Cinchoo ETL
             </a>
             - an open source library
            </p>
            <pre><code>public class MyDate
{
    public int year { get; set; }
    public int month { get; set; }
    public int day { get; set; }
}

public class Lad
{
    public string firstName { get; set; }
    public string lastName { get; set; }
    public MyDate dateOfBirth { get; set; }
}

static void ToJsonString()
{
    var obj = new Lad
    {
        firstName = "Tom",
        lastName = "Smith",
        dateOfBirth = new MyDate
        {
            year = 1901,
            month = 4,
            day = 30
        }
    };
    var json = ChoJSONWriter.Serialize&lt;Lad&gt;(obj);

    Console.WriteLine(json);
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Output:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>{
  "firstName": "Tom",
  "lastName": "Smith",
  "dateOfBirth": {
    "year": 1901,
    "month": 4,
    "day": 30
  }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Disclaimer: I'm the author of this library.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="35184335" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6201529" data-position-on-page="15" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="0" id="answer-35184335" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="35184335">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="0" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             0
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/35184335/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              Serializer
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code> public static void WriteToJsonFile&lt;T&gt;(string filePath, T objectToWrite, bool append = false) where T : new()
{
        var contentsToWriteToFile = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(objectToWrite, new JsonSerializerSettings
        {
            Formatting = Formatting.Indented,
        });
        using (var writer = new StreamWriter(filePath, append))
        {
            writer.Write(contentsToWriteToFile);
        }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Object
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>namespace MyConfig
{
    public class AppConfigurationSettings
    {
        public AppConfigurationSettings()
        {
            /* initialize the object if you want to output a new document
             * for use as a template or default settings possibly when 
             * an app is started.
             */
            if (AppSettings == null) { AppSettings=new AppSettings();}
        }

        public AppSettings AppSettings { get; set; }
    }

    public class AppSettings
    {
        public bool DebugMode { get; set; } = false;
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Implementation
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>var jsonObject = new AppConfigurationSettings();
WriteToJsonFile&lt;AppConfigurationSettings&gt;(file.FullName, jsonObject);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Output
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>{
  "AppSettings": {
    "DebugMode": false
  }
}
</code></pre>
           </div>
